[01-Oct-18 12:33 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Hi. We are building community for #marmara Chain now where we will have chains of post-dated cheques pegged to any currency, which will allow people to create their own money based on credit/debt in their selected currency. Thanks very much to @jl777c as being advisor to us in Discord group. These cheques have more than 200 billion USD market value now in Turkey alone. It is great value when especially considering not only the neighbouring countries but also any other country where post-dated cheques are/may be used in a chain structure. We will decide which technologies to continue with soon within our community. I am personally trying to promote Komodo technologies within our community to base the project on CC by Komodo. And I personally like the #verus mining algorithm which allows people to mine with CPUs. I believe this will help creating a huge community with the mineable coin on Marmara chain. We are currently working on defining the procedures for having a complete decentralization of whole processes which are currently held by banking and insurance institutions according to central laws. I invite all interested community members of Komodo into the Discord group to realize this project together.
https://discord.gg/8mBSKC7

[01-Oct-18 10:37 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
@polycryptoblog this is money creation based on credit/debt without interest/usury in a decentralized way when originally invented. But they end up with banks now. The only thing to do is to remove banks and other central decision making in the process. Banks involve during delivery of cheque books and when paying on due date. It is perhaps the most common instrument in Turkey and neighbouring countries. It enables ordinary people creating their own money based on credit/debt. It works same as banking with the exception of many circulation and no interest/usury fixed to it. When you get a loan from bank, it creates money out of thin air. And that money is destroyed when it is paid back. But since nobody creates the interest the borrower becomes slave to bank with compound interest rate. The bank created money only circulates between bank and borrower. Actually government bonds are same. They borrow money from banks and make us pay (modern slavery).

[02-Oct-18 12:06 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
It is a kind of chain/link of trust where people transfer trust to the next in the link. If you are not the last one in the link you are safe. Btw, the default rate is much lower than bank credit. If you think of laws enforcement and collaterals requirement by banks in case of bank loans, this is surprising. Isn't it?


[02-Oct-18 12:34 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
I think it works like this: it always happens between two persons who know each other. There is always trust. It is not completely anonymous. It happens during business where buyer and receiver knows each other very well. Suppose @jl777c writes a cheque for me to pay on say 1.1.2019. I know that @jl777c will keep money on his account on specified date not to put me into the trouble. @jl777c also knows that I may be the last person in the link and if no money exists in the account I will be in trouble. Of course, he will not feel well, either if I am the last one in the link. He will always assume that I may be the last one. Therefore,  @jl777c will not probably do something to harm me. Now suppose I have the cheque. I will be able to give this only to one who will have trust on me. He knows me not @jl777c. So trust has been transferred to me. We should remember that these cheques are used in real economy to buy and sell things among always two persons. They do not simply go from one location to another. Even if it goes, it always happens between two persons who trust each other. I think this is one of the main reasons why they work well.


[02-Oct-18 12:36 PM] jl777c#5810

[02-Nov-18 05:13 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
We have conducted our Workshop and analyzed the problem from Law, Business, Technology and Road Map points of view. We discussed important design criteria  that we decided based on invaluable discussions with @jl777c. I am very happy to announce that we have a consensus in our community to go with Komodo technologies. This decision is very important since we can find Ethereum developers more easily in Turkey. But we believe that the highly challenging problem of individual money creation by people based on credit/debt in completely decentralized manner could only be solved with Komodo technologies in the easiest way. We are planning to write a paper why we have chosen Komodo. The problem is not only having a blockchain version of analog trust chain of post-dated cheques and promissory notes any more. It is very clear to us that we can easily offer together to World a decentralized self-assured way of creating fiat money based on credit/debt in a trustful network. We have already a use-case with 200 billion usd market only with post-dated cheques. We want to expand it to general money creation based on debt as a complete alternative to banking system which creates fiat money based on credit/debt. Our difference is that we will have no slavery with the interest applied in banking credits as well as circulation of credits among many people while bank credit happens only between bank and borrower. We invited officially @jl777c to be advisor to project and we are honoured that he kindly accepted invitation. We invite all good developers and frontiers of Komodo community to our founding team to make this possible.
Regards

[05-Nov-18 12:35 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Actually Marmara Chain system may be used in any business. For example, We have cafes/canteens in university. Many of academics do not carry cash. We just say "please write it". Then when we have cash with us we just go and pay then the records are deleted. It was practiced in all small shops until recently. We called them "veresiye notebooks". It is a kind of small credit creation. As @jl777c rightly addressed with very simple GUI tools for mass adoption, we could use culture here very well and I am sure it is very similar in cultures such as India, Pakistan, Gulf and Balkans. Trust is essential within the culture of those areas.

[06-Nov-18 04:31 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
You are welcome! Thanks very much for your kindness. @Mylo For smaller communities, I am sure it will work much better. Marmara is actually based on trust between people. Therefore, we have virtually no need for privacy. Actually even privacy is a problem since nobody would accept a post-dated cheque if the original issuer is unknown. I checked the defaulting rates in Turkey. It is worse in greater cities but in small cities the defaulting rate is almost negligible. Since it is based on credibility/trust, and the reputation/credibility is all lost on default the people in small communities tend to pay it without delays/problems.

[01-Dec-18 03:01 PM] polycryptoblog#1173
How does mining tie into post dating cheques?


[01-Dec-18 10:48 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
@polycryptoblog It is not limited to only post-dated cheques any more. It is any credit creation. 50% of blocks will be timelocked always and 50% staking. Suppose I sell furniture worth 10k lira and you have no money except MARMARA immature coins. You write a post-dated cheque or create a credit with a future date on say 1 july 2019 worth of And you have immature coins spendable only after 1 july 2019 worth of 10k liras in MARMARA. There will be names on the system but even if I don't know you, I will sell this refrigerator to you without hesitation because of your immature coins after post-date.


[02-Dec-18 12:42 AM] jorian#4555
so the timelocking of funds relates to the credit creation part of MARMARA? timelocked block reward == post-dated cheque?


[02-Dec-18 02:02 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Yes. Timelocking is to help during redemption process against defaulting. Of course, there are also other factors. This is "a decentralized self-assured credit creation system" without any bank involvement.


[02-Dec-18 03:52 AM] GlorymanRTS#0512

[02-Dec-18 06:08 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
It is a trust based linking system shifting the trust from the first issuer to endorser. Then circulates between pairs of two sides who always trust the previous ones. Names of credit issuers are known to each other. It happens in business. They stamp on papers and put slgnatures.


[02-Dec-18 06:16 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
There are more. If there is not enough fund, the second node in the link is responsible. All nodes from top to bottom are responsible. They are visited and their funds are used to redeem. There is also 5% blockage for issuing a credit. And finally the 10% fund is used to clear. If the link fails they are all blacklisted especially the first node.

[23-Dec-18 01:44 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
@gcharang Thanks very much. I read the article. There is a common misunderstanding about the reality of money creation by banks. Many people are confused by the theory of Fractional Reserve banking (FRB)  system. I was also confused until I read the "lost century in Economics" by Professor Richard Werner. The main cause for misunderstanding is the publications made by Fed. The major one is "modern money mechanics". In reality, it is much easier to understand. FRB is fictitious and problematic to explain banks as intermediary institutions. In reality, banks just create credits when giving loans without need of any relending. And majority of money in circulation (97%)  is created as credit. In my opinion, banking could not be replaced by Blockchain unless credit function is solved in better way than banking system.

[25-May-19 11:55 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
@dimxy In Version 2.0, no need to have activated or boosted coins during issuance. It is money creation. But in Version 1.0, the issuer should have 100 % of coins locked. When the marmarabatonapproval is done, the activated/locked coins are transferred to boosted.


[25-May-19 12:01 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
In version 2.0, we will create credit as fiat currencies. It will be vadeli cheque (post-dated cheque) information on chain.


[25-May-19 12:11 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
In Version 1.0, we do not create money and no there is no fiat. Why would anyone give credit then if he/she cannot create credit? Well! We rely on the ability to generate MUCH MORE coins with boosted staking when locked in credit loops.


[25-May-19 12:13 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
25% of coins are produced with mining. The remaining is through activated and boosted.


[25-May-19 12:16 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
There are three types of coins as normal, activated and boosted ones. Boosted has three times more chance to find blocks during staking than activated coins*. Btw, staking needs activated or boosted, i.e. locked coins. 
* "three times more chance" is to be confirmed by @jl777c

[27-May-19 01:29 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
1. Yes. Settlement is actually cheque redemption at the date which is decided during issuance.
2. It is a real business even in Millennium edition (Version 1). Suppose I issue a credit of 600 MCL. When the first endorser (which is also holder) gets the baton, I buy goods and services for the amount of 600 MCL. But it does not leave my Wallet until redemption date. Furthermore, it is boosted so I get full power of staking. It is fully collateralized. At any stage, the zero defaulting occurs. However, as you discovered, the Version 1 is more miner friendly.
3. Yes, The millennium edition is simplified. The article explains the paper based analog chain Version of existing cultural system but Version 2 is a complete solution to nonredemption problem and other problems in paper version. 
4. In all versions, it works best with transfer of goods and services. But I admit that the Version 1.0 is more miner friendly since anyone can create to accounts and issue credit to himself/herself to use boosted staking. However, we want to spread Version 1 among community for exchange of real goods and services.

[27-May-19 03:57 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
The formula for risk share is same for all steps. It is Credit/(N-1). If there are 2 nodes in credit loop, the first is issuer and the second is holder. The issuer's 600 is locked in boosted. If there are 3 nodes, then 1st is issuer, the 2nd is endorser and 3rd is holder. So the credit risk is divided b/w issuer and endorser as 300. The issuer gets 300 back as normal coin while ensorser's 300 is locked first and then boosted when batonapproval happens. At each step, there is 100% collateralization.


[27-May-19 03:58 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
All previous nodes are responsible against the holder at the end date of credit loop.


[27-May-19 04:02 AM] dimxy#2587
Aha, seems this is not implemented yet when issuer should get back 300.


[27-May-19 04:09 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Yes. When the second node transfers the baton to the third one, the issuer gets back 300 as normal.


[27-May-19 04:11 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
So no staking ability for 300. That power passes to second one and the 3rd node becomes new holder. Holder is always last node.


[27-May-19 04:14 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
For real economic case, you would not give credit to anyone unless you received goods or services since you transfer your coin to the next node at the end.

[27-May-19 11:46 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626

[27-May-19 11:47 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626

[27-May-19 11:48 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626

[27-May-19 11:50 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
If issuer's activated fund is not enough, then the nodes in credit loop is visited in a top-to-bottom approach to settle the whole debt.


[27-May-19 11:51 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
If still not settled, the funds in  community layer are used. Supporters in community layer are called avalists.


[27-May-19 11:51 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
The third layer, the blockchain fund  is last resort of redemption.


[27-May-19 11:53 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626

[27-May-19 11:55 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
In summary, the Version 1 works on trustless nature of blockchain whereas the Version 2 is a trust based system.

[27-May-19 05:04 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
The earlier ones have more time to use the full staking power with more coins. The risk is reduced with each endorser added. If suppose there are 101 nodes in a credit loop, the node 100 pays only 1/100 of 600 to receive goods for 600 coins. [27-May-19 05:06 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626

[27-May-19 05:08 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626

[27-May-19 05:11 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626

[28-May-19 07:13 AM] dimxy#2587
Hello @B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner ,
Thank you once more for the explanations.
I also found this your note in the dev-chat transcript:
```At the due-date, all other nodes are responsible to the holder/last node starting from the credit creator first until the node before holder. If credit creator/issuer pays for holder, the credit is destroyed. If not paid, the non-redemption process starts. Either automatic or manual. In automatic, it is easier. The 5% blockage by credit issuer (if there is one) is transferred to holder/last node, then all timelocked coins belonging to credit issuer is used to pay for holder. If there is sufficient amount that is ok. The case is settled. Otherwise, all nodes in credit loop are visited one by one in sequence, and their timelocked coins are used to pay for holder. ```
From this I assume we need 2 rpcs:
1) marmara_settlement which tries to settle the baton with only issuer's funds: blockage + all timelocking funds are used to pay for holder
2) marmara_nonredemption which is executed if the first rpc was unsuccessful or partially successful. It visits all nodes and writes off their timelocked funds in equal fractions to pay to holder the remainder

[02-Jun-19 11:31 AM] dimxy#2587
Actually I have a concern how to manage lock-in-loop fund.
The updated document says that in settlement the system writes off the cheque amount from issuer and endorsers' both activated and lock-in-loop addresses, from top to bottom.
I think it is of course fair that issuer is responsible with all his funds: as he issued the credit and received goods for it then he should pay for it.
But is this fair for an endorser to pay with all his money if the issuer defaults? 
An endorser just gave goods and received goods, he actually gained none in total. Why should he be responsible with his both activated and locked coins?
Isn't it fair if all the endorsers in a loop should be equaly responsible with their locked-in-loop coins if the issuer defaults? 
That is, we could treat lock-in-loop coins as insurance fund which is spent only if the issuer defaults. 
So if he defaults, all endorsers would pay in equal proportion (and it would be easy to manage lock-in-loop fund).


[02-Jun-19 11:43 AM] jl777c#5810

[02-Jun-19 05:45 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
They are all collectively responsible to pay for the debt of holder who has given given goods but received nothing. The trust based version works from top-to-bottom. The trust and responsibility decrease with each new endorser. The most responsible one is issuer and the least is holder (actually no responsibility at all). Actually all are responsible against the holder. In Version 1, the earlier nodes will earn much more with boosted staking than the later nodes. Think of the endorser just before the holder in a loop with 100 nodes. The node 99, the last endorser is last contributor joining and earned not much but pays equally with the first endorser who had gained a lot until the last contributor.

[03-Jun-19 02:06 AM] dimxy#2587

Maybe your top-to-bottom schema is perfect and conforms the country law.
I just wanted to remind other possible reasons for endorsers: 
They all have put in lock-in-loop account the part of the collateral. In total it covers the debt for 100%. 
So each of them has prepared to risk that locked amount if case of the issuer defaulting. If the issuer defaults, the risk happens and all of them pay the lock-in-loop amount.

[03-Jun-19 12:01 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Thanks for asking. It is not very clear in document. Let me clarify. The baton transfer process always starts with marmarareceive first. That is started always by endorsers. In the first case, the first endorser starts process by using marmarareceive. The issuer should lock into activated to make marmaraissue. The baton is only created after the marmaraissue is done. But the baton is not transferred yet to first endorser. When the first endorser makes marmarabatonapproval, the baton is actually transferred to the first endorser and the activated coins are transferred to boosted.


[03-Jun-19 12:01 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626

[03-Jun-19 12:04 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
And for later nodes, just replace the marmaraissue with marmaratransfer.


[03-Jun-19 12:07 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Please remember. These operations happen after they were sitting and drinking tea and finally making handshaking for the deal.


[03-Jun-19 12:08 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Unless baton is approved by endorser the baton is not transferred.


[03-Jun-19 12:09 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626

[03-Jun-19 12:17 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
The coins remaining in activated is not a problem if baton is not transferred since the node can always use that later for issuing/endorsing new credits.


[03-Jun-19 12:30 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
@dimxy In the original design of Version 1 , 100% collateralization is possible at any stage. You can use Credit/(N-1) share for each one to pay for the settlement at the end. No need to go from top to bottom in Version 1. I had told that top-to-bottom for Version 1 after @jl777c said it would be problem with performance when there are too many nodes in credit loop. But since there is a common fund now in each credit loop, I assume there will not be a performance issue. The only thing to take care is to make sure each contributor gets earning/bonus relative to his/her share from power of 3x boosted staking. Earnings should be arranged with each holder coming into the credit loop.

[03-Jun-19 02:20 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
It will be same in both versions. It will be as follows for 3 nodes:-
Step 1: First endorser makes marmarareceive from issuer
Step 2: Issuer makes marmaraissue to first endorser (baton is created)
Step 3: first endorser makes marmarabatonapproval. Now baton is transferred to first endorser 
Step 4: holder makes marmarareceive from first endorser 
Step 5: first endorser makes marmaratransfer to holder
Step 6: holder makes marmarabatonapproval from first endorser. Now baton is transferred to holder.


Yes. In Version 2, there will be transactions before each marmarabatonapproval. At the initial step, the issuer might set escrow and also before every marmarabatonapproval between issuer/first endorser and endorser/holder there may be avalist transactions.


[03-Jun-19 03:06 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
There is chart for Version 2 in related requirements document. You can see that main differences are in escrow and avalist functions. There are also some additions for settlement and defaulting as well as Oracles functions.

[04-Jun-19 12:27 AM] dimxy#2587
Some notes about this:
```Step 1: First endorser makes marmarareceive from issuer
Step 2: Issuer makes marmaraissue to first endorser (baton is created)```
Technically, at the Step 2 Issuer would create a transaction to self (as the baton not yet passed to the endorser)

```Step 3: first endorser makes marmarabatonapproval. Now baton is transferred to first endorser```
Baton belongs to that pubkey who owns the utxo with it
So at the beginning of this step 3 baton is still owned by the issuer.
And in order to transfer the baton to the endorser I believe we would need another rpc method which should be called by the issuer.
I'm afraid we could not transfer the baton with marmarabatonapproval as it is called by the first endorser who does not own the baton yet and therefore cannot transfer it to himself.

[04-Jun-19 04:43 AM] dimxy#2587
Actually in the current implementation baton is created in the first marmaraissue

'R':  this is marmarareceive
 vins normal
 vout0 approval to senderpk (issuer or owner of baton)
 
 'I'    marmaraissue
 vin0 approval from 'R'
 vins1+ normal
 vout0 *baton* to 1st receiverpk
 vout1 marker to Marmara so all issuances can be tracked (spent when loop is closed)
 
 'T'  marmaratransfer
 vin0 approval from 'R'
 vin1 baton from 'I'/'T'
 vins2+ normal
 vout0 *baton* to next receiverpk (following the unspent baton back to original is the credit loop)

[20-Jun-19 11:28 AM] dimxy#2587
I think you need the following steps (on a fresh chain):
1) run 2 nodes without -gen -genproclimit parameters
2) on both nodes run getnewaddress and then validateaddress to get pubkeys
3) restart both nodes with -pubkey parameters and still without  -gen -geproclimit
4) on the first node run `setgenerate true 1`
5) wait for 3-4 blocks mined
6) on the first node run `marmarainfo 0 0 0 0` and ensure that there are activated coins
7) restart both nodes with params:
staked node (first) with `-gen -geproclimit=0`
second  node `-gen -genproclimit=$(nproc)`

[25-Jun-19 02:24 AM] dimxy#2587
on the pubkey2 node we first-time call `marmarareceive pubkey1` and then `marmaraissue pubkey2` on the pubkey1 node
then on the pubkey3 node we call second time `marmarareceive pubkey2` and then `marmaratransfer pubkey3` on the pubkey2 node

[26-Jun-19 11:48 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Great. It is going very  well.
1. What about boosted coins? Do they get 3x staking with boosted?  
2. Do we lock boosted in common fund? In the first case, the  PK1 should have 3x boosted staking. In the second case, both PK1 and PK2 should have 3x boosted staking with half (credit/(n-1))
3. Is settlement automatic?  Or do we need to make marmarasettlement manually?


[27-Jun-19 12:05 AM] Paro#7842
hi @dimxy


[27-Jun-19 12:08 AM] dimxy#2587
@B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner  
1. Yes, boosted coins take 3x multiplier in staking
2. We lock boosted coins on an 1of2 address that is unique to each credit loop and common (shared) for all loop's participants. But each utxo in a loop is marked by the pubkey who made this utxo. So we know what part of a loop fund belongs to which endorser and use this in the calculation of staking value. 
3. Settlement is automatic and is executed by a miner. There are some implications from this:
- anyone can now execute settlement
- it is now a problem to move the baton after the settlement (as it is stated in the requirements doc) because the baton is on the holder pubkey and anyone who does the settlement can't spend it


[27-Jun-19 12:09 AM] dimxy#2587
hi @Paro

[28-Jun-19 03:04 AM] dimxy#2587
LCL values are empty because they are null before the test and should be clear after the settlement (the table shows the status after the settlement). So the results are correct (as I understood the algorithmğŸ˜€ )
Total credit amount was 10 coins. After the settlement those 10 coins eventually were sent to pk3 normal.
For pk1 its activated account decreased by 10 coins and normal account increased by 5 coins. These 5 coins were sent to its normal when the look-in-loop amount was redistributed between pk1 and pk2 at the moment when the baton was sent to pk3.
For pk2 its activated amount is decreased by 5 coins (which he donated to the loop).

The settlement now is automatic and is started by any miner.
(And it creates a problem: the miner who started the settlement cannot send the baton to the issuer as required by the document. The baton is on the holder's pubkey and the miner cannot spend it)

[28-Jun-19 10:51 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626

Then this blockchain fund may be used for transferring baton to issuer as well. Is it difficult or impossible technically?


[29-Jun-19 04:58 AM] dimxy#2587
The 'global address' is a feature common for every komodo cc contract. This address might be used for various purposes. It is like a shared account. Although anyone might spend funds from this address this spending is controlled by the validation code.
Currently in marmara this address is used for storage of markers, that is, small amounts on this address which allow to enumerate the transactions which have such an utxo. By this we can find all 'marmaraissue' transactions for open credit loops.
The marmara validation code will allow to spend such markers for the settlement transactions and by this close the credit loop.
And yes we can store marmara's backup fund on this adddress too.


[29-Jun-19 05:14 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Can we start a new test chain such as MCL1 with the common blockchain fund? This is stated in requirements document as the third layer for protection against nonredemption. In case of insufficient normal funds but with enough activated/boosted, this fund may be utilized. Perhaps It may be utilized for transferring baton to issuer at the end when the credit loop expires.


[29-Jun-19 05:28 AM] dimxy#2587
Yes I think we can a new chain which would allow to use common fund to cover normal accounts with insufficient amounts on them.
To allow a miner to transfer the baton we should change the way of baton's storage: now the baton is on the holder's pubkey and no one except him can move the baton. To allow a miner to move it we should store the baton on some special address (like 1of2 address of endorser pk+global pk) which would allow both endorser and miner to move the baton. Plus we will need to write very carefully the validation code to prevent moving the baton in all cases except the settlement.


[29-Jun-19 06:19 AM] dimxy#2587
But from the previous messages I understood we may avoid returning the baton to the issuer after the settlement. How will it be used after it is returned to the issuer?
If we can avoid it I'd suggest maybe not to change this. It seems to me the storing the baton on the loop participant's pubkey is simple solution and does not involve additional transaction validation


[29-Jun-19 07:03 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626

[29-Jun-19 07:33 AM] dimxy#2587
I'd say this is not about which one is easier. It is more like what is needed. I noticed in the chat messages that we are going to use moving the baton back to the issuer to indicate that the loop is closed. But we also have another feature for the same task - the marker. We already do spending the marker at the settlement to closed the loop. Maybe this will solve that task. 
But if not, and we need to move the baton to the issuer for some other reasons, let's do this.

Yes the common fund feature will be implemented, I cannot see any problems to do this.

[05-Jul-19 08:23 AM] dimxy#2587
I have made a version with a special test parameter -marmara-test-pubkey where generated activated coins are sent to (in the repo).
To test staking multipliers I suggest preparing for the test 2 PoS nodes and 2 non-mining nodes.
On the 1st PoS node set up a credit loop for some amount (and lock all activated coins)
On the 2nd PoS node provide the same amount of activated coins (and no lock-in-loop)
On both the PoS nodes set -marmara-test-pubkey to pubkeys from the 2 non-mining nodes correspondingly.
on those non-mining nodes you will be able to see generated coins for staked utxos with 1x and 3x multipliers

[05-Jul-19 01:37 PM] dimxy#2587
The idea is to have a test environment providing results that are easy to check.
The test should show that lock-in-loop coins provide 3x chances for staking vs 1x for activated coins.
To check this it will be good if there are 2 staking nodes in the test, one with activated coins and another with lock-in-loop coins.
Both amounts should be equal, to make it possible to check the ratio easy.

As PoS nodes generate new activated coins they would interfere with initially set coins for staking.
That's why a temp parameter was added to komodod to send generated coins to other addresses.
so we could send them to any 2 non-mining nodes (for example pk1 and pk2)


[05-Jul-19 01:43 PM] dimxy#2587
so we should have 2 PoS nodes (setgenerate=0), on the first of them let's set up 500 activated coins and for the 2nd node 500 lock-in-loop 
Credit period should be long enough, for example 24 hours 
on both nodes we need add temp params:
-marmara-test-pubkey=pk1
-marmara-test-pubkey=pk2
and we could monitor generated coins on the pk1 and pk2 nodes with marmarainfo (and check the ratio)

[15-Jul-19 02:12 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
I was with @Paro and @zeki yesterday. They are making black box tests. I also joined in some of the tests personally. Let me try to translate our concern @dimxy and @jl777c .  We made tests with the codes before the addition of blank parameters from Version 2. I think there is a fundamental problem as far as I  see from test results. We need to clarify it. When someone has coins in LCL, he/she should be staking 3x than normal activated. Now it seems to work like this. Suppose I have 40000 activated and no coin in LCL. It works with normal staking power. But supposse I have 10 coins only in LCL and I have 40000 in activated. And someone has  40000 coins in LCL but only 10 coins as activated. He can produce more even if the other person has more in LCL. I think it currently looks at the person if he/she has coins in LCL and prodcues from the activated ones not based on the LCL. LCL wallet address is only one address common to all and actually not stakeable.  Therefore, we don't encourage the real credit creators. People just need to lock something to get full 3x power of staking. If we summarize, we just need to lock something  in LCL to have 3x staking. The 3x staking is based on activated ones and not the coins  in LCL. This is what we see from the system. I think the problem may be solved by making  a stakeable address such as  "myLCLAmount" similar to "myActivatedAmount". Both  "myLCLAmount" and "myActivatedAmount" should stake simulatenously according to their contents.  I think "myAmountOnActivatedAddress-old" may be deleted. It is not needed any more. It was used to collect the latest 16 activated ones when we were having activated coins  between 3 months to 2 years. Now all coins are activated at a maximum height. I don't know if I could explain the concern well ?@Paro


[15-Jul-19 02:34 AM] dimxy#2587
If we are concerned with that low LCL amount produces small number of blocks (and big amount of activated coins will consume most of the blocks generation) we might disable staking on activated and enable only on LCL coins. But if the total LCL amount for that whole chain is low the staking might be unstable.
Alternatively we could change the  multiplier for LCL

[15-Jul-19 03:12 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
@Paro I think we need to look at the coding part to explain our concern. Black box tests are not enough.


[15-Jul-19 03:17 AM] dimxy#2587
the code is fully open. You might be concerned with LCL implementation. LCL is implemented as a shared account for the system to be able to spend it and redistribute amount between the endorsers (as the doc states). But each LCL utxo is marked with the pubkey who owns this part. So for staking only those utxo are picked up that are marked with the miner's pubkey. So this is a complete equivalent for myLCLaccount.


[15-Jul-19 03:26 AM] dimxy#2587
you could ask about any part of the code and I can clarify it.
Most of the code (rpc and helpers, opretun creation functions) is in cc/marmara.cpp.
Staking extensions are in komodo_bitcoind.h file
calling creation of miner's transactions is in miner.cpp file, 
this creation func, which calls MarmaraRunAutoSettlement, is in komodo_gateway.h

{Reactions}
ğŸ‘ 

[15-Jul-19 03:38 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Do the staking extensions in komodo_bitcoind.h  also include LCL part?


[15-Jul-19 03:59 AM] dimxy#2587
the algorithm of adding staking utxo is in cc/marmara.cpp, MarmaraGetStakingUtxos which is called from the komodo_bitcoind.h


[15-Jul-19 04:00 AM] dimxy#2587
it enumerates both activated utxos then LCL utxos for the mypubkey (which is miner's pk)
Applying of the multipliers is in the cc/marmara.cpp MarmaraGetStakeMultiplier function, this function is called back from komodo_bitcoind.h, func komodo_txtime2

(komodo_bitcoind is a common src file, it itself contains little app logic and provides only callbacks which extend the basic komodo functionality for specific marmara features. The logic is in marmara.cpp)

[20-Jul-19 10:13 AM] dimxy#2587
this is how I calculate 3x:
```
uint32_t komodo_txtime2(uint64_t *valuep,uint256 hash,int32_t n,char *destaddr)
{
...
if ( n < tx.vout.size() )
    {
        int32_t stakemultiplier = GetStakeMultiplier(tx, n);
        *valuep = tx.vout[n].nValue * stakemultiplier; 
    ...
    }
}
```
so there is GetStakeMultiplier() func, it calls MarmaraGetStakeMultiplier() func

[06-Aug-19 10:49 AM] dimxy#2587
I'm rethinking about issues with staking.
Actually my 3-node marmara chain is stalling. This shows itself as blocks are generated with long delays and there are messages in log:
```640 seconds until elegible, waiting. 
600 seconds until elegible, waiting.
...```
(That is, more than 10 min waiting for an utxo.)
Our other developers suggested that this is because not enough utxos for staking.
Indeed, in non-marmara chains we usually use utxo splitting on 64 addresses (this is about normal coins of course).
In our marmara chain we have not yet implemented such splitting for activated coins, and I'm thinking why we need this.
As I understand JL correctly, in large marmara chains we would not need splitting as there will be many user addresses and segids will be filled up naturally.
In fact this splitting on 64 segids is needed for small chains, while we do not have many addresses yet.
So I am implementing this splitting of activated coins for small test chains to run stable 
(And we should understand it would affect rewards generation: of course, split activated coins will have much more advantage over non-split lock-in-loop coins). 

Seems, this feature will be used also in the production chain on its early stage to make it stable.
And it should be some transition period until enough addresses appear on chain because the initially split coins would affect new users' activated and lock-in-loop coins rewards. 
(That is, the initially split coins should be taken off as enough other addresses are on the chain)

[08-Sep-19 07:43 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
@Paro How is the test for 3x boosted staking going? @dimxy


[08-Sep-19 11:12 AM] dimxy#2587
I believe the boosted staking works but I think we did not verify it mathematically. It is not easy because of segids: to make the chain stable we split activated coins on 64 segids. So if we usually create only one loop for test its boosted coins would be staked rarely (as most of staking would be coming on the activated coins that are split on 64 segids). 
I think we might develop some not very complicated rpc which would enumerate PoS generated coins and output some statistics on them, like if this is activated or boosted staking, which address, total amount. Then we probably could see overall staking results.
Probably we would need to create loops for some specified time (to get enough statistic data) and allow to set a period for the getting statistic for the rpc.
I think it might need at least 1000 PoS blocks generated (with boosted utxo in the chain) to see the expected results as all 64 segid utxos will be used for staking and we will need to wait for many blocks to see that the single boosted utxo have been picked for staking at least several times.

[15-Sep-19 12:09 PM] dimxy#2587
Hello,
I have created a new rpc ```marmaraposstat begin-height end-height``` that returns PoS statistics: stake addresses and how much coins were generated for each of them. It is also shown if an address is boosted and how many stake txns were generated for it.
-----
Also I found and fixed a bug with normal coinbase scriptpubkey generation.
------
So I suggest the following way to research boosted coins usage:
- update all nodes with the new version from my repo
- create a long credit loop (for 5000 blocks). The loop amount should be approximately equal to the amount of activated coins on each segid. Do not add any new endorsers to the loop, just wait.
- note the height where this loop was created
Now for boosted coins a stake multiplier of 100x is set in the code.
When enough blocks are passed we can run marmaraposstat  from the height where the loop was created till the chain tip and look into the stat.
If the algo works correct we would see in the marmaraposstat output that for the boosted address there are more stake tx and coins generated than for other non-boosted addresses

[17-Sep-19 04:27 AM] dimxy#2587
@Paro I updated code in my repo (https://github.com/dimxy/komodo/tree/marmara-v1-1-opret-v2), fixed some issues with staking for boosted coins.
I recommend starting a new chain to check boosted coins PoS generation.

for a new chain, to see how boosted coins generate blocks, make sure that all the segids have equal utxo values, for example make them with command 'marmaralock64 640 1', this will create 64 segids with one utxo in each of 10 coins.
Then make a loop also for 10 coins and for 5000 blocks till it matures.
Then you might periodically call `marmaraposstat 0 0` to see what address generated most of the blocks.
You may find the lock-in-loop address in marmaraposstat output with 'IsBoosted: true' tag.

(Note that I temporarily disable activated coinbases generation for even block for they do not contaminate PoS staking)

{Reactions}

[17-Sep-19 04:29 AM] dimxy#2587
Actually for boosted coins PoS preference is done very simply: its value just multiplies by 100x (for test, actual will be 3x)
so 10 boosted coins will be accounted as 1000 coins in staking in this should be always the winner if all other segids utxos have only 10 coins

[03-Nov-19 07:20 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
I am very busy at the moment and I could not follow pegs and gateway. But as far as I understand it might solve a common problem that are happenning with post-dated cheques use. I think @jl777c will give idea since he knows very well how post-dated cheques work in Turkey. 

The problem is this. Suppose you have a post-dated cheque from someone with a long redemption date say 1.1.2021. I am holder of cheque now. I cannot wait until that date and I cannot sell it for goods. Can I exchange it for KMD, VRSC, BTC etc? What happens at the moment in Turkey? The person goes to a bank and sells it for cheaper price. Actually bank becomes holder. They call it breaking a cheque. But in reality, the cheque, i.e. the credit loop is not broken. A bank becomes holder, i.e. waits until the redemption date. It is simply using another asset/coin instead of GOODS. Can we do that with pegs and gateways? @Paro may share the case as a picture since I cannot upload the picture.

[03-Nov-19 07:24 PM] Paro#7842
@B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner example 

receive Post-dated Cheques
``` ./komodo-cli -ac_name=MCLTEST marmarareceive pkendorser batontxid 55 KMD "kmd-walletaddress"```
accept endorser 
```./komodo-cli -ac_name=MCLTEST marmaratransfer pkholder batontxid```
in this way, "Post-dated Cheques" will be passed to a new endorser.
In order to get the check, the person needs to have a KMD coin.
I still haven't made plans about how KMD or other coins will be formed.
I guess it needs to be multi-wallet.
In this way, "Post-dated Cheques" can be swap safely and conveniently.
on foot with this thought. can be developed in different ways.

[04-Nov-19 11:43 AM] dimxy#2587
I could not achieve the required results in my tests for coin generation for activated and boosted:
My test conditions were to create activated coins evenly on 64 segids and lock the same amount for a long loop. The multiplier was set to 100x. So I had the even amount of activated and boosted coins and big multiplier for test results to be easy to interpret.
Then I waited for 10K blocks and checked number of blocks generated in each segid (there is a getlastsegidstakes rpc to get PoS block count in segids). I hoped the boosted coins would generate much more blocks but it seemed the generated block number was the same on all segids (so seems the multiplier or the way how I applied it did not provide the expected staking effect).
I asked kmdlabs for help with this.
We might repeat a similar test on your chain providing very accurate test start conditions to have test results easy verifiable and observe the whole picture of PoS (maybe I did something wrong or misinterpreted the test results)

[04-Nov-19 12:10 PM] dimxy#2587
PoS enumerates 64 segid and looks for utxo for staking. On large chains where there are many addresses they will be present in each segid naturally.
For our test chains we need to generate addresses for all segids to provide PoS to work correctly (otherwise it could be stalling)
I temporarily have turned off generation of activated coins (in coinbase) in order to they do not contaminate the initial test conditions (so the initial number of utxo would persist throughout the whole test) - so we can observe how many PoS block are generated with the multiplier and without it.
Mass load tests are required I totally support this!

[15-Dec-19 05:17 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Odoo is an Open Source ERP system with more than 4 million users globally and very suitable for all SMEs while it is easily scalable to large organisations.  Odoo needs to be customized in Turkey especially in accordance with financial regulations. 

We can develop trust based features in Marmara Version 2 by merging Odoo ERP with Marmara Credit Loops. When considering the users of post-dated Cheques as being mostly SME businessmen, Marmara has a good chance of penetrating into ERP market in Turkey by having a good addon/module integrating trust based features of Marmara with ERP systems. Therefore, we established â€œOdoo Turkeyâ€ Discord group. We invite you there, I think it will have huge effect if Komodo is involved/integrated in ERP business. Btw, before entering into Odoo, we had a thorough research for selection of best Open Source ERP system at a large institution to start with and Odoo was the best among many alternatives. 

We invite Odoo and/or Komodo Developers who can help in integration of Marmara Chain with Odoo.

https://discord.gg/zzJgxCh

[10-Jan-20 02:20 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
Can we use boosted staking idea in Marmara for Energy production systems? Let us call it WattCoin. Suppose you have solar panel, Wind Turbine etc to produce Energy. We will measure Energy production in a device and use that as a metric for staking. Rewarding somehow will be mostly based on Energy production. Similar to Marmara, we can have 25% mining and 75% staking based on boosted staking with hardware connection to smart Energy devices. There are smart devices for measuring the Watt power from electric production units. If we can connect that to staking then we can solve problem. The coins representing Watt power can be transferred within credit Loops same as in MCL. I can transfer you some WattCoins with a post-dated value as Watt credits. We need electronic Engineers knowledgeable in Komodo blockchain to be involved in the process.

My old friend from New Zealand sent me something about protecting yourself from Corona Virus. Let me translate it.

Let me tell you a story leaked from the Chinese, they would recommend pure vitamin C to help prevent the outbreak in Italy. They say that tablet C vitamins sold in pharmacies are damaged by other chemicals in contact with air. So I went to a natural care clinic 10 years ago, they recommended me to take Ascorbic Acid (vitamin C), which was sold in white powder, because I had pain in my arm, I have been drinking two large glasses of filtered water in the mornings for a long time. I mix 4 teaspoons of this powdered ascorbic acid, I drink it by pouring water, I have not had a disease called flu for the last 10 years. Here, family doctors encourage people to get flu vaccines, especially for the elderly, for free, I have never received these vaccines, I do not. Now if I tweet this news, there may be no ascorbic acid in the market as we have seen in Cologne...

We have almost 4 seasons in Turkey in proper periods. And during winter, most of the food comes very rich in Vitamin C such as lemons, oranges, spinach etc. You can get Vitamin C naturally from these winter food.

Wish you a healthy life!

[18-Mar-20 08:07 AM] Paro#7842
Marmara Credit Loops (MCL) 

To the contrary belief, banks are not the sole institutions for creating money based on credit. In many countries all over the world, like banks, individuals are able to create money through post-dated cheques or promissory notes in a decentralized manner.

Inspired by the paper-based blockchain nature of these promissory notes and post-dated chequesâ€™ circulation, in the same analogy, Marmara Credit Loops Project aims to digitalize the blockchain while solving the problem of nonredemption of these tools. 

The early release of this Project, named as Version 1, solves the problem of non-redemption with 100% collateralization through trustless blockchain mechanism. 

The second version of the Project aims to solve the nonredemption problem based on a trust based blockchain system with the aid of a protective layered architecture of nodes in credit loop layer formed against defaulting. 

 https://youtu.be/hQYgDhSsHrI

{Embed}
Marmara Credit Loops
https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hQYgDhSsHrI

[30-May-20 02:22 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
@everyone  ``marmaraunlock``, i.e. the sister of ``marmaralock`` is coming to Marmara Credit Loops

I am happy to inform that we are bringing ``marmaraunlock`` into life on consensus level. That will need a hard fork at a certain height. Thanks to @dimxy, the core developer of MCL. He has finished the coding for ``marmaraunlock`` and we are testing it. We tried to make marmaraunlock before the hardfork height. The error message was just fine as below.
``./komodo-cli -ac_name=MCL marmaraunlock 1
{
  "result": "error",
  "error": "unlocking not available yet"
}
`` 
We will share the result after the hard fork height in test chain  is reached.

By ``marmaraunlock`` we will be getting rid of artificial credit loops in order people to take out activated coins. You will be able disactivate/unlock your active/locked coins with ``marmaraunlock``

[09-Jun-20 06:47 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
***Dear Marmara Credit Loops (MCL) Community,***
We have good news. We have finished the tests for the new consensus changes. We will be able to hardfork at the same time with Komodo NN hard fork. The community needs to update to the new Version. 

**What are the major changes in Credit Loops?**
As you know, Marmara Credit Loops were designed to be used in real economy with a market place worthing currently more than total crypto market with a size of post-dated cheques alone and in Turkey (please check for other countries). Here are the new consensus rules to boost MCL in real economy.
**1. The holders, i.e. the bearers of credits can benefit from 3x staking without locking any single coin in a loop. That means providers of goods and services will earn when they are selling.

2. There will be no coin locks and cuts from endorsers during a credit loop.

3. Endorsers will not get any reward from 3x staking.

4. Ä°ssuers and holders will be able to do 3x staking throughout life cycle of a loop.

5. The old credit loops will work normally as before and get settled when they mature. However, you cannot transfer them.

6. ``marmaraunlock`` function will allow to unlock your activated funds without the need of creating an articial loop**


[10-Jun-20 03:20 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
@everyone 
*Marmara v.1.0.2 Hardfork*

Change log

- "marmaraunlock" was added. No need to create credit loops to open/unlock activated coins.
- No cut off and locking for endorsers
- Endorsers cannot make 3x staking.
- Both issuer and holder can make 3x staking throughout credit Loop life cycle. Holder needs no locking for 3x staking.
- Old loops will continue 3x staking until settlement but cannot get transferred.


*PLEASE UPDATE THE VERSION.!*

---------------------------------------------------
https://github.com/marmarachain/Marmara-v.1.0
---------------------------------------------------
komodod,komodo-cli (only Linux)
http://www.marmara.io/guifiles/Linux-MCL-HF.zip

Hardfork DATE : 06/24/2020 @ 2:00pm (UTC)
---------------------------------------------------
For Ubuntu servers and PCs
```
1.
wget http://www.marmara.io/guifiles/Linux-MCL-HF.zip
2.
unzip Linux-MCL-HF.zip
3. 
sudo chmod +x komodod komodo-cli fetch-params.sh
4. 
./fetch-params.sh
5.
./komodod -ac_name=MCL -ac_supply=2000000 -ac_cc=2 -addnode=37.148.210.158 -addnode=37.148.212.36 -addnode=46.4.238.65 -addressindex=1 -spentindex=1 -ac_marmara=1 -ac_staked=75 -ac_reward=3000000000 &

```
Guide : https://github.com/marmarachain/MarmaraChain/blob/master/win-mcl.md

*Video (Turkish).*
https://youtu.be/PzFoptvCz6w

*LIBRARIES FOR FIRST TIME SETUP*
-------------------------------
```sudo apt-get update
sudo apt-get upgrade -y
sudo apt install ufw
sudo ufw --version
echo y | sudo ufw enable
sudo apt-get install ssh
sudo ufw allow "OpenSSH"
sudo apt-get install build-essential pkg-config libc6-dev m4 g++-multilib autoconf libtool ncurses-dev unzip git python zlib1g-dev wget bsdmainutils automake libboost-all-dev libssl-dev libprotobuf-dev protobuf-compiler libgtest-dev libqt4-dev libqrencode-dev libdb++-dev ntp ntpdate software-properties-common curl clang libcurl4-gnutls-dev cmake clang -y
sudo apt-get install libsodium-dev```

[22-Mar-21 05:04 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
One of the millennia generations has explained MCL as they understand it.. Many Thanks.
** You can grasp the MCL best when you use it in real shopping. So what is MCL? Why should we shop with MCL instead of shopping with USD? After reading the story below, replace every place you see USD with MCL and read it again.

Bob, who wants to buy a new phone, takes the path of the seller, Alice. The phone he likes is $ 1000 and he goes to the cash register to buy it. Bob will be able to pay in two ways. With the first option, he can pay $1000 in advance. In the second option, Alice tells Bob that he can pay with a 6-month credit loop. According to this system, $1000 will be locked in a reward pool between Bob and the Alice. After 6 months, $1000 will be transferred to Alice. Alice says that as long as $1000 is locked between them, both of them can generate USD from this pool.

When Bob realizes that he can pay $1000 and generate over $1000 for 6 months, he happily wants to pay with the second method and buys the phone with a 6-month credit loop.

Later Alice remembers that she had to pay her supplier of $ 1000 for a few electronic items. But Bob is the only customer who has come to his shop for a long time and there is no money left in the cash register. Remembering that the credits in the credit loop can be transferred, Alice transfers/endorses the $1000 credit in the loop to the supplier. The credit loop is no longer between Bob and the Alice, but between Bob and the supplier. Now, the supplier can generate money over $1000 with Bob.

So why do we shop with MCL, not USD? Have we ever been able to generate USD from anything we bought with USD? No. MCL makes it possible for you to generate MCL both while receiving and making payments. In this system, both the buyer and the seller earn rewards. It also allows you to shop using the credit loops of a previous purchase, even if you don't have any MCLs in your pocket. **

[24-Mar-21 01:01 PM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
We are trying to peg it to goods and services. But we are not at a stage yet to put enough of goods backing. Currently it seems to be pegged partially to Komodo prices on AtomicDEX. My assumption is that it will be balanced somehow with the prices of goods and services. It will first reflect the local prices since majority of selling happens in Turkey. With @jl777c, We had discussed the fluctuation for the first year. I think the inflation rate and fluctuation is normal for first year since it is difficult to adopt first years due to lack of easy to use tools. We have Marmara Connector to make loops easily but it runs on Linux. The majority of people use Windows. Now @Aklix and @ryilmaz in the team are working on Marmara Connector for Windows version. But of course, later we definitely need mobile version since postdated cheques happen on fly. We need to conduct credit loops with mobile. It is a longterm project. We are still in an early stage.

Did you know that the economy was not bad When banks were closed in total around one year between 1966 and 1976 in Irish Banking Crisis? The longest period was in 1970 for more than 6 months at one closure. People invented the post-dated cheques, an analog version of Marmara credit loops $MCL. https://www.mortgagebrokers.ie/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Antoin-Murphy-Money-in-an-economy-without-banks-The-case-of-Ireland-bank-strike-paper.pdf

[03-Jan-22 02:00 AM] B. GÃ¼ltekin Ã‡etiner#0626
**INTERNATIONAL ROSCA DAYS**
We will start international ROSCA days soon to start to learn the power of Credit Loops. I hope that **these ROSCAs will also promote business on international level.**

Every two weeks, you need  1000 MCL as Credit to send to the group member in queue. In one case, you will make credit loop request to all other members.

**RULES**
1. A ROSCA group is constructed first with 10 members at maximum.
2.  A draw is made to decide the order. 
3. Each person in accordance with the draw makes a Credit Loop request worth to 1000 MCL with 6 months maturity from each person getting 9000 in total. If you are first in the group, you will have a total of 9000 MCL as credit loops immediately.
4. You can simply circulate/endorse a previous credit in a loop. 
5. Since this is also a learning activity, the transactions can happen only as Credit loop.
6. We will have private dm group on Discord for each ROSCA group.

**You can just click in the channel link below  if you want to join**

This is how ROSCAs work in Turkey. Originally, the women in Turkey started the ROSCA days as GOLD days. The idea is used in many businesses from housing to buying cars without any need of credits from banks. https://yabangee.com/gold-day-recipes-delicious-eats-for-a-day-of-socializing-and-giving-gold/
